## Class ZoomType

**Package:** `com.osmb.api.item`

**Type:** Class

**Extends/Implements:** extends Enum<ZoomType>

### Methods

#### `values()`

**Returns:** `ZoomType[]`

Returns an array containing the constants of this enum class, in the order they are declared.

**Returns:** an array containing the constants of this enum class, in the order they are declared

#### `valueOf(String name)`

**Returns:** `ZoomType`

Returns the enum constant of this class with the specified name. The string must match exactly an identifier used to declare an enum constant in this class. (Extraneous whitespace characters are not permitted.)

**Parameters:**
- `name` - the name of the enum constant to be returned.

**Returns:** the enum constant with the specified name

**Throws:**
- IllegalArgumentException - if this enum class has no constant with the specified name
- NullPointerException - if the argument is null

#### `rasterH()`

**Returns:** `int`

#### `rasterW()`

**Returns:** `int`

#### `offsetX()`

**Returns:** `int`

#### `offsetY()`

**Returns:** `int`

**Returns:** `int`

#### `getRowIncrement(int row)`

**Returns:** `int`

#### `getCore()`

**Returns:** `ScriptCore`

#### `search(Set<Integer> itemIdsToRecognise)`

**Returns:** `ItemGroupResult`

Scans an item group for specified items, automatically handling group visibility and expansion. This method will: Check if the item group is visible (attempting to open it if expandable) - returns null if not visible Search all slots in the group for the specified item IDs Return detailed results including the best match for each found item Visibility Handling: For Expandable groups: Attempts to open if closed (requires core.getFinger() to be non-null) For regular components: Only checks visibility (does not attempt to make visible) Returns null immediately if the group cannot be made visible

**Parameters:**
- `itemIdsToRecognise` - The IDs of the items to recognise.

**Returns:** An ItemGroupResult containing search results, or null if the group isn't visible.

**Throws:**
- IllegalArgumentException - If itemGroup doesn't implement Component or Expandable

#### `getBoundsForSlot(int slot)`

**Returns:** `UIResult<Rectangle>`

#### `getMissclickBoundsForSlot(int slot)`

**Returns:** `UIResult<Rectangle>`

#### `getItemGroupBounds()`

**Returns:** `UIResult<Rectangle>`

Gets the complete bounding rectangle for an entire ItemGroup

**Returns:** Rectangle representing the bounds (x, y, width, height). If the ItemGroup's Component is not visible, then will return UIResult.isNotVisible().

#### `getSlotCoordinates(int slotNumber)`

**Returns:** `UIResult<Point>`

## ItemGroupResult

**Package:** `com.osmb.api.item`

**Type:** Class

Represents the result of scanning an item group in the game UI, containing information about found items, slot occupancy, and various query methods for item retrieval.

**Extends/Implements:** extends Object

### Methods

#### `getOccupiedSlots()`

**Returns:** `Set<Integer>`

#### `getFreeSlots()`

**Returns:** `int`

Counts the number of free slots in the item group.

**Returns:** Number of unoccupied slots

#### `getFreeSlots(Collection<Integer> itemsToIgnore)`

**Returns:** `int`

Counts the number of free slots in the item group, excluding the provided items. Accepts any Collection of item IDs to ignore.

**Parameters:**
- `itemsToIgnore` - Collection of item IDs to ignore when counting free slots

**Returns:** Number of unoccupied slots

#### `getOccupiedSlotCount()`

**Returns:** `int`

Counts the number of occupied slots in the item group.

**Returns:** Number of occupied slots

#### `contains(int itemID)`

**Returns:** `boolean`

Checks if the item group contains an item.

**Parameters:**
- `itemID` - The ID of the item to check

**Returns:** true if the required amount is found, false otherwise

#### `contains(int itemID, int amount)`

**Returns:** `boolean`

Checks if the item group contains at least the specified amount of an item.

**Parameters:**
- `itemID` - The ID of the item to check
- `amount` - The minimum required amount

**Returns:** true if the required amount is found, false otherwise

#### `getAmount(int... itemIDs)`

**Returns:** `int`

Calculates the total amount of a specific or multiple items in the group.

**Parameters:**
- `itemIDs` - The IDs of the items to count

**Returns:** Total stack amount of the specified item

#### `getAmount(Collection<Integer> itemIDs)`

**Returns:** `int`

Calculates the total amount of specific items in the group.

**Parameters:**
- `itemIDs` - The collection of item IDs to count

**Returns:** Total stack amount of the specified items

#### `getItem(int... itemIDs)`

**Returns:** `ItemSearchResult`

Gets the first found instance of an item in the group.

**Parameters:**
- `itemIDs` - The IDs of the items to find

**Returns:** The first ItemSearchResult matching the ID, or null if none are found

#### `getItem(Collection<Integer> itemIDs)`

**Returns:** `ItemSearchResult`

Gets the first found instance of an item in the group.

**Parameters:**
- `itemIDs` - The collection of item IDs to find

**Returns:** The first ItemSearchResult matching any ID, or null if none are found

#### `getAllOfItem(int itemID)`

**Returns:** `List<ItemSearchResult>`

Gets all instances of a specific item in the group.

**Parameters:**
- `itemID` - The ID of the item to find

**Returns:** List of all ItemSearchResults matching the ID

#### `getAllOfItems(int... itemIDs)`

**Returns:** `List<ItemSearchResult>`

#### `getAllOfItems(Collection<Integer> itemIDs)`

**Returns:** `List<ItemSearchResult>`

#### `getOneOfEachItem()`

**Returns:** `List<ItemSearchResult>`

Gets one representative of each unique item found in the group.

**Returns:** List containing one ItemSearchResult per unique item ID

#### `containsAny(int... itemIDs)`

**Returns:** `boolean`

#### `containsAny(Collection<Integer> itemIDs)`

**Returns:** `boolean`

#### `containsAll(Collection<Integer> itemIDs)`

**Returns:** `boolean`

Checks if the item group contains all of the specified items (at least one of each).

**Parameters:**
- `itemIDs` - The collection of item IDs to check

**Returns:** true if all specified items are present, false otherwise

#### `getRecognisedItems()`

**Returns:** `List<ItemSearchResult>`

Gets all found items in the group.

**Returns:** Set of all ItemSearchResults

#### `isFull()`

**Returns:** `boolean`

Checks if the group is completely full

**Returns:** true if all slots are occupied

#### `isEmpty()`

**Returns:** `boolean`

Checks if the group is completely full

**Returns:** true if none of the slots are occupied

#### `getSlotForItem(int itemID)`

**Returns:** `int`

Gets the slot number containing the first occurrence of the specified item.

**Parameters:**
- `itemID` - The ID of the item to locate

**Returns:** The slot number containing the item, or -1 if not found

**Throws:**
- RuntimeException - if the item group is not visible

#### `getSlotsForItem(int itemID)`

**Returns:** `Set<Integer>`

Gets all slot numbers containing the specified item.

**Parameters:**
- `itemID` - The ID of the item to locate

**Returns:** Array of slot numbers containing the item, or empty array if none found

**Throws:**
- RuntimeException - if the item group is not visible

#### `getSelectedSlot()`

**Returns:** `Integer`

Gets the slot index of the currently selected item in the item group. The selected item is typically visually indicated by a white outline in the game UI.

**Returns:** An integer representing the selected slot, or null if no slot is selected.

#### `isSlotOccupied(int slot)`

**Returns:** `boolean`

#### `getRandomItem()`

**Returns:** `ItemSearchResult`

#### `getRandomItem(int itemID)`

**Returns:** `ItemSearchResult`

#### `getRandomItem(int... itemIDs)`

**Returns:** `ItemSearchResult`

#### `getRandomItem(Collection<Integer> itemIDs)`

**Returns:** `ItemSearchResult`

#### `getOccupiedSlots(Collection<Integer> itemsToIgnore)`

**Returns:** `Set<Integer>`

Gets all occupied slots in the item group, excluding specified items. This method is useful for determining which slots are occupied by items that are not in the provided collection of items to ignore.

**Parameters:**
- `itemsToIgnore` - Collection of item IDs to ignore when checking occupied slots

**Returns:** Set of occupied slot numbers, excluding those containing ignored items

#### `equals(ItemGroupResult otherItemGroupResult)`

**Returns:** `boolean`

Checks if this ItemGroupResult is equal to another ItemGroupResult. This method performs a deep comparison of two ItemGroupResult objects by examining: ItemGroup equality (must be the same group) Slot occupancy maps (size and values must match exactly) ItemSearchResult collections (all items must have matching IDs and slot positions) Two ItemGroupResults are considered equal if they represent the same item group with identical slot occupancy states and contain the same recognised items in the same slots. The comparison is order-independent for the item collections.

**Parameters:**
- `otherItemGroupResult` - The ItemGroupResult to compare with this instance

**Returns:** true if both objects represent the same item group state with identical slot occupancy and recognised item distributions, false otherwise or if the parameter is null

## ItemManager

**Package:** `com.osmb.api.item`

**Type:** Class

The `ItemManager` interface defines the contract for managing and interacting with items inside a Component which implements an ItemGroup (eg. Inventory) It provides methods for retrieving item definitions, searching for items, managing item groups, and performing actions like dropping items.

### Fields

- `static final ToleranceComparator ITEM_TOLERANCE_COMPARATOR`

### Methods

#### `itemGroupVisible(ScriptCore core, ItemGroup itemGroup)`

**Returns:** `boolean`

Checks if an item group is visible and, if the parent implements expandable, ensures it is open.

**Parameters:**
- `itemGroup` - The item group to check.

**Returns:** `true` if the item group is visible and open (if applicable), otherwise `false`.

**Throws:**
- IllegalArgumentException - If the item group does not implement `Component` or `Expandable`.

#### `getItemDefinition(int itemID)`

**Returns:** `ItemDefinition`

Retrieves the definition of an item by its ID.

**Parameters:**
- `itemID` - The ID of the item to retrieve.

**Returns:** The ItemDefinition corresponding to the item ID.

#### `getItemDefinitions()`

**Returns:** `List<ItemDefinition>`

Retrieves a list of all item definitions.

**Returns:** A list of ItemDefinition objects.

#### `scanItemGroup(ItemGroup itemGroup, Set<Integer> itemIds)`

**Returns:** `ItemGroupResult`

Scans an item group for specified items, automatically handling group visibility and expansion. Key Features: Selective Scanning: Only searches for items matching the provided IDs for optimal performance Complete Slot Tracking: Records all occupied slots regardless of requested items Smart Visibility Handling: Automatically manages expandable/visible states Why Provide Item IDs? RuneScape contains tens of thousands of possible items. Rather than inefficiently checking every possible item: You specify exactly which items to look for We still track all occupied slots in the container Results will include both your requested items and general slot occupancy data Visibility Handling: For Expandable groups: Attempts to open if closed (requires core.getFinger() to be non-null) For regular components: Only checks visibility (does not attempt to make visible) Returns null immediately if the group cannot be made visible Operation Flow: Visibility Check: Attempts to make the group visible if needed Slot Scanning: Checks every slot while tracking: Occupied status (regardless of item ID) Best matches for your specified items Currently selected slot Result Compilation: Returns both targeted matches and general slot information

**Parameters:**
- `itemGroup` - The container to scan (inventory, bank, etc.)
- `itemIds` - The specific items to search for (empty list will still return slot occupancy)

**Returns:** Detailed scan results including: - ItemSearchResult Matches for your specified items - Complete slot occupancy data - Selected slot information OR null if container can't be made visible

**Throws:**
- IllegalArgumentException - If the itemGroup is invalid

#### `getSlotForPoint(ItemGroup itemGroup, Point p)`

**Returns:** `UIResult<Integer>`

Retrieves the slot index for a specific point in the item group.

**Parameters:**
- `itemGroup` - The item group to check.
- `p` - The point to check.

**Returns:** A UIResult containing the slot index if the point is within a slot, otherwise `null`.

#### `isItemAt(SearchableItem image, int x, int y)`

**Returns:** `ImageSearchResult`

#### `getItemImage(int id, int amount, ZoomType zoomType, int borderColor, int rasterBackgroundColor, int backgroundColor)`

**Returns:** `ItemImage`

Retrieves an item image for the specified item ID.

**Returns:** An Image of the specified item ID.

#### `isItemAt(SearchableItem image, int x, int y, boolean checkBorder)`

**Returns:** `ImageSearchResult`

#### `findLocation(boolean checkBorder, Rectangle bounds, SearchableItem... items)`

**Returns:** `ItemSearchResult`

Finds the first location of the specified items within a given rectangular area on the screen. Only use this method if there is no item group available, as it is slower than using an item group.

**Parameters:**
- `checkBorder` - Will check for the black border around the item - if false, it will not check for the border.
- `bounds` - The rectangular area to search within. If null, searches the entire screen.
- `items` - The items to search for.

**Returns:** The first `ItemSearchResult` found, or null if none found.

#### `findLocations(boolean checkBorder, Rectangle bounds, SearchableItem... items)`

**Returns:** `List<ItemSearchResult>`

Finds locations of specified items within a given rectangular area on the screen. Only use this method if there is no item group available, as it is slower than using an item group.

**Parameters:**
- `checkBorder` - Will check for the black border around the item - if false, it will not check for the border.
- `bounds` - The rectangular area to search within. If null, searches the entire screen.
- `items` - The items to search for.

**Returns:** A list of `ItemSearchResult` objects representing the found items.

#### `findLocations(Rectangle bounds, SearchableItem... items)`

**Returns:** `List<ItemSearchResult>`

Finds locations of specified items within a given rectangular area on the screen. Only use this method if there is no item group available, as it is slower than using an item group.

**Parameters:**
- `bounds` - The rectangular area to search within. If null, searches the entire screen.
- `items` - The items to search for.

**Returns:** A list of `ItemSearchResult` objects representing the found items.

#### `getItem(int itemId, boolean border)`

**Returns:** `SearchableItem[]`

Retrieves an array of SearchableItem objects for a specific item ID.

**Parameters:**
- `itemId` - The ID of the item to retrieve.
- `border` - Whether to include a border around the item images.

**Returns:** An array of SearchableItem objects.

#### `getItemImage(int id, int amount, ZoomType zoomType, int backgroundColor)`

**Returns:** `Image`

Retrieves the image of an item with the specified parameters.

**Parameters:**
- `id` - The ID of the item.
- `amount` - The amount of the item.
- `zoomType` - The zoom type for the image.
- `backgroundColor` - The background color for the image.

**Returns:** The Image of the item.

#### `getItemImage(ItemDefinition itemDefinition, ZoomType zoomType, int backgroundColor)`

**Returns:** `Image`

Retrieves the image of an item using its definition.

**Parameters:**
- `itemDefinition` - The definition of the item.
- `zoomType` - The zoom type for the image.
- `backgroundColor` - The background color for the image.

**Returns:** The Image of the item.

#### `getItemName(int itemID)`

**Returns:** `String`

Retrieves the name of an item by its ID.

**Parameters:**
- `itemID` - The ID of the item.

**Returns:** The name of the item, or `null` if the item definition is not found.

#### `isStackable(int itemID)`

**Returns:** `boolean`

Checks if an item is stackable by its ID.

**Parameters:**
- `itemID` - The ID of the item.

**Returns:** `true` if the item is stackable, otherwise `false`.

#### `getNameForItemID(int itemID)`

**Returns:** `String`

#### `getItem(int itemId, boolean border, int rasterBackgroundColor)`

**Returns:** `SearchableItem[]`

#### `getItem(int itemId, boolean border, ToleranceComparator toleranceComparator, ColorModel colorModel)`

**Returns:** `SearchableItem[]`

#### `getItem(int itemId, boolean border, ToleranceComparator toleranceComparator, ColorModel colorModel, ZoomType zoomType)`

**Returns:** `SearchableItem[]`

#### `getItem(int itemId, boolean border, ToleranceComparator toleranceComparator, ColorModel colorModel, ZoomType zoomType, int backgroundColor)`

**Returns:** `SearchableItem[]`

#### `overrideDefaultComparator(int itemID, ToleranceComparator comparator)`

Overrides the default comparator for a specific item ID.

**Parameters:**
- `itemID` - The ID of the item to override.
- `comparator` - The new comparator to set, or null to remove the override.

#### `overrideDefaultColorModel(int itemID, ColorModel colorModel)`

Overrides the default color model for a specific item ID.

**Parameters:**
- `itemID` - The ID of the item to override.
- `colorModel` - The new color model to set, or null to remove the override.

#### `getComparator(int itemID)`

**Returns:** `ToleranceComparator`

Retrieves the comparator for a specific item ID.

**Parameters:**
- `itemID` - The ID of the item.

**Returns:** The `ToleranceComparator` for the item, or the default (23,23,23) if no override is set.

#### `getColorModel(int itemID)`

**Returns:** `ColorModel`

Retrieves the color model for a specific item ID.

**Parameters:**
- `itemID` - The ID of the item.

**Returns:** The `ColorModel` for the item, or the default (RGB) if no override is set.


---

## ItemSearchResult

**Package:** `com.osmb.api.item`

**Type:** Class

Represents a found item from a ItemGroup search, with additional metadata and interaction capabilities. Extends ImageSearchResult to include visual matching information.

**Extends/Implements:** extends ImageSearchResult

### Fields

- `public static final int M_TEXT_COLOR` - Color value for 'M' (million) text in stack amounts
- `public static final int K_TEXT_COLOR` - Color value for 'K' (thousand) text in stack amounts
- `public static final int YELLOW_TEXT_COLOR` - Color value for yellow text in stack amounts

### Methods

#### `isSelected()`

**Returns:** `boolean`

#### `getSlot()`

**Returns:** `int`

**Returns:** The ItemGroup slot number (-1 if equipment)

#### `getEquipmentSlot()`

**Returns:** `EquipmentTabComponent.Slot`

**Returns:** The equipment slot (null if inventory item)

#### `getId()`

**Returns:** `int`

**Returns:** The item ID

#### `getRandomPointInSlot()`

**Returns:** `UIResult<Point>`

Gets a random point within the item's bounds for clicking

**Returns:** UIResult containing a random point or visibility status

#### `getTappableBounds()`

**Returns:** `UIResult<Rectangle>`

Gets the clickable bounds of the item

**Returns:** UIResult containing the bounds rectangle or visibility status

#### `getItemGroup()`

**Returns:** `ItemGroup`

**Returns:** The item group this belongs to (null if equipment)

#### `getStackAmount()`

**Returns:** `int`

**Returns:** The stack amount of the item

#### `getItemSlot()`

**Returns:** `int`

**Returns:** The ItemGroup slot number (alias for getSlot())

#### `interact(String... options)`

**Returns:** `boolean`

Interacts with the item using specified options

**Parameters:**
- `options` - The interaction options (e.g., "Use", "Drop")

**Returns:** true if interaction was successful

#### `interact(MenuHook menuHook)`

**Returns:** `boolean`

Interacts with the item using a custom menu hook

**Parameters:**
- `menuHook` - the menu hook to use for interaction

**Returns:** true if interaction was successful

#### `interact()`

**Returns:** `boolean`

Default interaction with the item (single click)

**Returns:** true if interaction was successful

#### `interact(boolean bypassHumanDelay)`

**Returns:** `boolean`

Default interaction with the item (single click)

**Parameters:**
- `bypassHumanDelay` - if true, skips the human delay (Not recommended unless you know what you're doing)

**Returns:** true if interaction was successful

#### `toString()`

**Returns:** `String`


---
